studies, youth programs, and community outreach. We also host educational events, interfaith dialogues, and activities promoting unity and spiritual growth.</p><p>Join us in strengthening faith and fostering community connections.</p></div></div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_button_module_wrapper et_pb_button_7_wrapper"><a class="et_pb_button_7 et_pb_button et_pb_bg_layout_light" href="/donate-now" target="" data-icon="" data-icon-tablet="" data-icon-phone="" rel="">Donate Us</a></div></div></div></div><div class="et_pb_section_10 et_pb_section et_section_regular" id="marriage"><div class="et_pb_row_15 et_pb_row et_pb_gutters1"><div class="et_pb_column_20 et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough"><div class="et_pb_divider_2 et_pb_divider_hidden et_pb_space et_pb_divider_position_top et_pb_module"><div class="et_pb_divider_internal"></div></div></div><div class="et_pb_column_21 et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et-last-child et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough"><div class="et_pb_text_27 et_pb_text et_pb_bg_layout_light et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_module"><div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h4></h4></div></div><div class="et_pb_text_28 et_pb_text et_pb_bg_layout_light et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_module"><div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2>Marriage</h2></div></div><div class="et_pb_text_29 et_pb_text et_pb_bg_layout_light et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_text_align_center-tablet et_pb_module"><div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>The Islamic Center of Macomb (ICM) offers marriage services to support couples in beginning their journey together in accordance with Islamic principles. Our services include Nikah ceremonies, pre-marital guidance, and community support to help couples build strong, faith-centered relationships.</p><p>For more information or to schedule a Nikah ceremony, please contact us. We are here to assist you in creating a blessed and meaningful start to your marital life.</p></div></div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_button_module_wrapper et_pb_button_8_wrapper"><a class="et_pb_button_8 et_pb_button et_pb_bg_layout_light" href="/donate-now" target="" data-icon="" data-icon-tablet="" data-icon-phone="" rel="">Donate Now</a></div></div></div></div><div class="et_pb_section_11 et_pb_section et_section_regular" id="funeral"><div class="et_pb_row_16 et_pb_row et_pb_gutters1"><div class="et_pb_column_22 et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et-last-child et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough"><div class="et_pb_text_30 et_pb_text et_pb_bg_layout_light et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_module"><div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h4></h4></div></div><div class="et_pb_text_31 et_pb_text et_pb_bg_layout_light et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_module"><div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2>Funeral</h2></div></div><div class="et_pb_text_32 et_pb_text et_pb_bg_layout_light et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_text_align_center-tablet et_pb_module"><div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>The Islamic Center of Macomb (ICM) offers support and guidance during times of loss, ensuring Islamic funeral rites are performed with care and respect. Our services include assistance with funeral arrangements, ghusl (ritual washing), shrouding, and Janazah (funeral prayer).</p><p>We are here to provide compassion and support to grieving families while adhering to Islamic traditions. Please contact us for assistance or more information.</p></div></div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_button_module_wrapper et_pb_button_9_wrapper"><a class="et_pb_button_9 et_pb_button et_pb_bg_layout_light" href="/donate-now" target="" data-icon="" data-icon-tablet="" data-icon-phone="" rel="">Donate Now</a></div></div></div></div><div class="et_pb_section_12 et_pb_section et_section_regular" id="shahada"><div class="et_pb_row_17 et_pb_row et_pb_gutters1"><div class="et_pb_column_23 et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough"><div class="et_pb_divider_3 et_pb_divider_hidden et_pb_space et_pb_divider_position_top et_pb_module"><div class="et_pb_divider_internal"></div></div></div><div class="et_pb_column_24 et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et-last-child et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough"><div class="et_pb_text_33 et_pb_text et_pb_bg_layout_light et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_module"><div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h4></h4></div></div><div class="et_pb_text_34 et_pb_text et_pb_bg_layout_light et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_module"><div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2>Shahada</h2></div></div><div class="et_pb_text_35 et_pb_text et_pb_bg_layout_light et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_text_align_center-tablet et_pb_module"><div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>The Islamic Center of Macomb (ICM) warmly welcomes individuals interested in embracing Islam.
